## CHAPTER X11-14

RECEIVABLES REPORT MENU

### Introduction

The purpose of this job is to list the your options for creating accounts receivable
reports. The reports include:

- three reports of chronological age

— a detailed list of all information concerning your receivables
— asummary list of information conceming your receivables
— alist of all customers that have exceeded their limit credit

~ alist of the credit conditions of your receivable

~ alist of all customers without statements

— avolume list

— an insurance expiration report

— areceivables master report

### Contents

2 X11-14 ¢ RECEIVABLES REPORT MENU RELEASE 2.1
ERASE 2

### Entrance Screen

O From the Receivables Menu (X1-1), select option 14, Receivables Reports
Menu and press [Enter].

Oi If the Receivables Security Gate appears, enter your division code and security
code and press [Enter]. The Receivables Reports Menu appears:

 

+ Aged Receivables Summary Report » Receivables Exceeding Credit Limit
. Aged Receivables Detail Report . Receivables Credit Definition List
+ Aged Receivables Collection Report - Receivables Without Statement List
» List of Receivables (Summary) 10. Receivables Volume List

- Receivables Credit List 22. Receivables Master Report

Menu appears.


ACCOUNTING X11-14 ¢ RECEIVABLES REPORT MENU 3
eS IS OOo Eee a SY

### Receivable Reports Menu Options

The Receivables Reports Menu includes the following options:

1. Aged Receivables Summary Report

Select this option to print a list of the selected receivables with their current and
past balances, and a summary of general ledger account balances by the age of the
teceivable.

2. Aged Receivables Detail Report

Select this option to print a complete list of all information concerning the
selected receivables with their current and past balances and a summary of general
ledger account balances by the age of the receivable.

3. Aged Receivables Collection Report

Select this option to print a complete list of the receivables having transactions
that have exceeded the limit entered in the field “Number Of Days Where The
Collection Becomes Critical” under the option Receivable Maintenance (X11-2),
or the number of days entered in the selection screen for this report.

4. List of Receivables (Summary)
Select this option to print an information report of all receivables or for selected
Teceivables.

5. List of Receivables (Detail)
Select this option to print a complete report of all information for all receivables
or for selected receivables.

6. Receivables Credit List
Select this option to print an information report on receivables with credits. This
Teport includes a list of all running transactions for the selected receivables.

7. Receivables Exceeding Their Credit Limit List

Select this option to print an information report on receivables that have exceeded
their credit limit. This report displays the customer balance, the credit limit, and
the difference between these two amounts.

8. Receivables Credit Definition List
Select this option to print an information report on the credit definitions for each
selected receivable.


4 X11-14 ¢ RECEIVABLES REPORT MENU RELEASE 2.1
ee SSSSSSSSSSSMMES IESE SET

9. Receivables Without Statement List

Select this option to print a list of customers for whom you do not print
statements. These customers are set up with the value “N” (No) in the “Print”
field under the menu item Receivable Maintenance (X11-2).

10. Receivables Volume List

Select this option to create a list, by customer, of the total receivables for the
previous 12 months. The list includes, for each customer, total dollar amount of
all receivables, number of transactions, and average transaction amount. The list
also includes a grand total of receivables, number of transactions, and average
transaction amount for your business.

11. Insurance Expiration Report
Select this option to create a report of customer’s insurance policies for
tental/leasing, sorted by expiration date.

12. Receivables Master Report

Select this option to create a detailed report of all your receivable accounts.
At the end of the report is a summary or Recap which contains totals and
percentages for all Receivable Accounts, the total dollar amounts 30 days, 60
days, 90 days, and over 120 days past due, and the total number of Receivable
Accounts 30, 60, 90, and over 120 days past due.

## CHAPTER X11-15

CALCULATE RECEIVABLES AGE

### Introduction

This option calculates aging for all receivables accounts for all divisions from
their transaction dates to the current session date. To calculate the age fora
particular receivable account, go to the Receivables Menu (X1-1), option 1,
Receivables Inquiry. The age of all receivable accounts is calculated automatically
during the end of day procedure.

### Contents

2 X11-15 « CALCULATE RECEIVABLES AGE RELEASE 2.1

### Entrance Screen

O From the Receivables Menu (X1-1), select option 15, Calculate Receivables
Age and press [Enter]. The Calculate Receivables Age Confirmation screen

appears.

Nw EQUIPMENT SALES CALCULATE RECEIVABLES AGE X11F00-02
Division A
*** Confirmation ***

This option recalculates the aging of all receivable customers
for all your divisions. Make sure no accounting jobs (DU) are
running before you initiate this option.

A message will be sent to this screen when the calculation is
completed.

Cmdl-End Enter-Continue

 

Screen A: Calculate Receivables Age Confirmation.

CALCULATE RECEIVABLES AGE

0 To determine whether accounting jobs are running, exit the procedure by
pressing (Cmd1] - End. On a command line, type D U and press [Enter]. If
there are no jobs that begin with "X1" in the "Proc" field, you can continue.

O From the Calculate Receivables Age Confirmation screen, if no accounting
jobs are running, to calculate the receivables age, press [Enter].

When the calculation is complete, you will receive the following message:

The receivables aging calculation has completed.

O To return to the Receivables Menu, press [Cmd1] - End.

## CHAPTER X11.14-1

AGED RECEIVABLES SUMMARY REPORT

### Introduction

The purpose of this job is to allow you to create a report of all or selected
receivables with their past and current balances, as well as a summary by general
ledger account according to the age of the balance of the receivable.

You can select the receivables for this report by the general ledger account, the
group code or the address number. You can sort the report by customer name or
address number. Also, you can print the report for any general ledger month or
you can print a report for the current month.

their addresses, and transaction numbers by the date or the number of the invoice.

print a report for the current month.

## CHAPTER X11.14-3

AGED RECEIVABLES COLLECTION REPORT

### Introduction

The purpose of this job is to allow you to create a detailed Teport of receivables in
selected categories having transactions past due and that have exceeded the limit
entered in the field, “Number Of Days That Makes Collection Critical” in
Receivables Maintenance (X1 1-2) or the number of days entered in the Selection
screen for this option.

You can select the receivables for this Teport by the general ledger account, the
group code or the address number. You can sort the report by customer name or
address number. You can sort transactions by invoice number or by date. Also,
you can print the report for any general ledger month or you can print a report for
the current month.

### Contents

     

Select By Address Number. a
PRINT AGED RECEIVABLES COLLECTION REPORT... .eescssesesesceesees

Receivables Collection Report and press [Enter].

O Ifthe Receivables Security Gate appears, enter your division code and security
code and press [Enter]. The Aged Receivables Collection, Selection screen
appears:

ACCOUNTING X11.14-3 e AGED RECEIVABLES COLLECTION REPORT 3

 

PRINT AGED RECEIVABLES COLLECTION REPORT

Parameter Selection

C1 Enter a parameter in the “Enter Number Of Days That Makes Collection
Critical” field. This field allows you to include in the report all customers that
have critically past due invoices, including those who have no definition in the
field “Number Of Days That Makes Collection Critical” in Receivables
Maintenance (X11-2). If a customer does have a definition under Receivables
Maintenance, then this definition will be used to include the customer in the
Teport. If you want to include only customers having a definition in
Receivables Maintenance, leave the “Enter Number Of Days That Makes
Collection Critical” field blank.

0 Enter one of the following parameters to determine how customers will be
sorted on the report:
1 =Sort by customer name
2 = Sort by customer address number

C1 Enter one of the following parameters to determine how transactions will be
entered on the report:
1 = Enter transactions by invoice date
2 = Enter transactions by invoice number

O Enter one of the following parameters to determine how customers will be
selected for the report:
1 = Select by general ledger account or include all customers
2 = Select by group code
3 =Select by address number

C1 To continue, press [Enter], or to exit the procedure without printing the Aged
Receivables Collection Report and return to the Receivables Report Menu
(X11-14), press [Cmd1] - End.

customer. The amount prints in dollars without

(X5-1) and Receivables Inquiry (X11-1). To set up

## CHAPTER X11.14-7

### Introduction

The purpose of this job is to allow you to create a report of customers who have
gone over their credit limit. You can choose to print all the receivables ora
specific receivables. The report displays the customer balance, the credit limit,
and the difference between these two amounts.

Descriptions of fields of the report:

### Field Description

Sorted by The sort customers parameter entered in the
Selection screen (name or address number).

Selection by The selection parameter entered in the Selection
screen (general ledger account, group code, or
address number).

Adr. # The address number of the customer.

Name The name of the customer.

Balance The account balance for the customer.

Past Due The number of days the account is past due.

Limit The credit limit set for the customer. To set up your

system to stop Point Of Sale billing for customers
that have exceeded their credit limit, see the
directions in the “Credit Limit” field in Receivables
Maintenance (X11-2).

Credit Code #1 The first credit code, followed by its description.
Credit codes are set up in Receivables Maintenance
(X11-2).
Credit Code #2 The second credit code, followed by its description.
Total The total of the balances for the selected customer
accounts.
Number of Customers The number of customers included in the report.
Past Due Amounts Summary:
Current The current balance of all selected accounts.
Over 30 Days The total of balances past due by 31 to 60 days.
Over 60 Days The total of balances past due by 61 to 90 days.
Over 90 Days The total of balances past due by 91 to 120 days.
Over 120 Days The total of balances past due by 121 days or more.

## CHAPTER X11.14-9

RECEIVABLES WITHOUT STATEMENT LIST

### Introduction

The purpose of this job is to allow you to create a list of receivables which will
not normally print statements. These receivables have a value of “N” (No) in the
“Print?” field under the option, Receivable Maintenance (X11-2). You can choose
to print all the receivables or selected receivables.

## CHAPTER X11.14-10

RECEIVABLES VOLUME LIST

### Introduction

The purpose of this job is to allow you to create a list, by customer volume, of
your total receivables for the previous 12 months. The list includes, for each
customer, total dollar amount of all receivables, number of transactions, and
average transaction amount. The list also includes a grand total of receivables,
number of transactions, and average transaction amount for your business.

### Contents

  

ENTRANCE SCREEN
THE RECEIVABLES VOLUME LIST

## CHAPTER X11.14-11

INSURANCE EXPIRATION REPORT

### Introduction

The purpose of this job is to allow you to create a report of customer’s insurance
policies for rental or leasing, sorted by expiration date. .

## CHAPTER X11.14-12

RECEIVABLES MASTER REPORT

### Introduction

The purpose of this job is to allow you to create a detailed report of all of your
Receivable Accounts. The report may be run at any time without having to do
Monthly Billing. At the end of the report is a summary or Recap which contains:
— totals and percentages for all Receivable Accounts

— total dollar amounts 30 days, 60 days, 90 days, and over 120 days past due

- total number of Receivable Accounts 30, 60, 90, and over 120 days past due

### Contents

ENTRANCE SCREEN
THE RECEIVABLES MASTER REPORT...
RECAP BY GENERAL LEDGER ACCOUNT REPOR

+ Aged Receivables Detail Report - Receivables Credit Definition List
+ Aged Receivables Collection Report 3. Receivables Without Statement List
- List of Receivables (Summary) 10. Receivables Volume List

- List of Receivables (Detail) 11. Insurance Expiration Report

. Receivables Credit List 12. Receivables Master Report

23. Return To Receivables Menu

Ready for option number or command (mdi-Resume Job

Screen A: Receivables Reports Menu

O From the Receivables Reports Menu (X11-14), select option 12, Receivables
Master Report and press [Enter]. If the Receivables Security Gate appears,
enter your division code, select whether to print all divisions, enter your
security code and press [Enter]. The Receivables Master Report is placed on
the job queue.

O To retum to the Receivables Menu, press [Enter]. The Receivables Master
Report and Recap by General Ledger Account will print.
